# Store Release Notes

- [Now Assist Suite release notes](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ServiceNow/ServiceNowDocs/store/markdown/store-release-notes/sn-store-now-assist-suite-release-notes.md) -- Now Assist applications often function interdependently. Now Assist Suites help reduce runtime errors and upgrade issues by bundling compatible versions of Now Assist applications together.
  - [Now Assist Suite - June 2026 release notes](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/ServiceNow/ServiceNowDocs/store/markdown/store-release-notes/na-suite-rn-2026-06.md) -- The Now Assist Suite's version and compatibility information for June 2026.
